  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_69994c63-98ad-43ec-b751-5818d702a2fb'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

Ox found out later the boy hadn’t spoken in almost two years before that day, and that the boy belonged to a family who had moved into the house at the end of the lane.<br /><br />Ox was seventeen when he found out the boy’s secret, and it painted the world around him in colors of red and orange and violet, of Alpha and Beta and Omega.<br /><br />Ox was twenty-three when murder came to town and tore a hole in his head and heart. The boy chased after the monster with revenge in his bloodred eyes, leaving Ox behind to pick up the pieces.<br /><br />It’s been three years since that fateful day—and the boy is back. Except now he’s a man, and Ox can no longer ignore the song that howls between them.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3395344357" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2250964766861971013">this is the most unpopular opinion i've had in a hot sec,,,welcome to it<br/><br/>i initially picked this up bc the third book in the series features a couple with an ace character, and i want to read that SO bad, but after reading this i doubt i’ll ever make it there bc, woah boy, this was very much nooooot for me. and trust me, i am truly wavering on what to rate this bc i usually reserve one stars for books that have no redeeming qualities, but that’s not the case with this one. it’s got big found fami</span>
  <span id="freeText2250964766861971013" style="display:none">this is the most unpopular opinion i've had in a hot sec,,,welcome to it<br /><br />i initially picked this up bc the third book in the series features a couple with an ace character, and i want to read that SO bad, but after reading this i doubt i’ll ever make it there bc, woah boy, this was very much nooooot for me. and trust me, i am truly wavering on what to rate this bc i usually reserve one stars for books that have no redeeming qualities, but that’s not the case with this one. it’s got big found family excellence, there is a strong sense of setting, and i can totally see how people could get attached to these characters (they reminded me a lot of the crew from nora sakavic’s aftg series)<br /><br />however, this story is primarily a romance, and the entire relationship that developed between ox and joe made me wildly uncomfy. that age gap was a *choice* (basically, joe mated with ox when he was 10 and ox was 16. when joe was 17 and ox was 22 things started to get romantic and i??? don’t feel super right about that??) to be fair i’ve never loved romances where there is any substantial imbalance of power (age, status, occupation, etc.) but the fact that ox and joe met so young, essentially grew up together as family, and tHEN got together just really rubbed me the wrong way. not to mention, once their relationship had begun, joe was intensely possessive and primal (big sjm vibes) again, proprietary romances haven’t been a thing i enjoy for a loooong time, so this could just be a me thing, but i heard some things on this audiobook that...kinda made me wanna unzip my skin and crawl right out of it (rowan whitethorn WHOMST (i’m joking (mostly))) <br /><br />please enjoy a few quotes that make this point for me:<br /><br />“i had to stop myself from tearing you apart...you’re amazing and beautiful, and sometimes i want to put my teeth in you just to watch you bleed. i want to know what you taste like…i don’t want anyone to touch you ever again…”<br /><br />“there are times when all i can think of is marking you so that everyone knows who you belong to. to carve my name into your skin so you can never forget me...i have to protect what’s mine.” <br /><br />“i want to claim you. i want to give you scars with my claws. i want my teeth imbedded in your neck....you’re mine. no one else can have you. no one else can be with you...you hear me ox? not ever...and i’ll kill anyone who thinks they can take you away from me.”<br /><br />i think that about covers it bc idk how to go on after typing out some of that shit. no judgement if u like this one, but it just was too much for my lil brain<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2250964766861971013" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1781581031" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1781581031" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1781581031?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog">Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=favorite-couple">favorite-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=mm-or-lbgtq">mm-or-lbgtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=grief">grief</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=loved-you-since-childhood">loved-you-since-childhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=gives-good-grovel">gives-good-grovel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1781581031" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7158678525659110606"><b>5 "Candy Canes and Pine Cones and Epic and Awesome" Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478100276ra/21031553.gif' width='465' height='229' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I originally read this book in preparation for a giveaway over on the blog; but rest assured, said giveaway had NOTHING to do with me giving this bad boy 5 big ones.<br/><br/>If it had sucked, I would have rated it however many "suck" stars it deserved, written a semi-diplomatic "this thing sucked" review...<br/><br/>And then still done my blog-wife duty and shamelessly plugged the giveaway.<br/><br/>But thank <i>fuck</i> I didn't have to do that. <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478100857ra/21031651.gif' width='498' height='262' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Because this thing was awes</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7158678525659110606" style="display:none"><b>5 "Candy Canes and Pine Cones and Epic and Awesome" Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478100276ra/21031553.gif" width="465" height="229" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I originally read this book in preparation for a giveaway over on the blog; but rest assured, said giveaway had NOTHING to do with me giving this bad boy 5 big ones.<br><br>If it had sucked, I would have rated it however many "suck" stars it deserved, written a semi-diplomatic "this thing sucked" review...<br><br>And then still done my blog-wife duty and shamelessly plugged the giveaway.<br><br>But thank <i>fuck</i> I didn't have to do that. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478100857ra/21031651.gif" width="498" height="262" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Because this thing was awesome. </b><br><br>Before this book, I had never read - or even heard of - T.J. Klune, quite frankly, but a few weeks ago, my non-PNR-reading blog-wife Maria, said, "OMG Val, you just HAVE to read this awesome M/M PNR book I just read. It was fucking fabulous."<br> <br>Well, okay, that wasn't <i>exactly</i> what she said...<br><br>But that's what I heard. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478100857ra/21031652.gif" width="245" height="233" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But anyexaggeration, homie Maria was right.<br><br>I loved this thing. <br><br>As I said, I've never read anything by T.J. Klune before, so I'm not sure if this book is an example of his general writing style or just his writing style for this book. Either way...<br><br>It's <i>very</i> different.<br>And it just really worked for me here. <br><br>The entire story is told from the POV of our main character, Ox.<br><br>Ox lives in the country in the middle of Green Creek aka Nowhere, Oregon. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478104435ra/21032226.gif" width="245" height="141" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah, exactly. <br><br>Anyway, Ox's father tells him he is stupid and the kids at school call him a "retard."<br><br>But really, Ox is just a simple boy with simple wants and needs and a heart of fucking gold.<br><br>And when I say "simple," I mean that the way he sees the world and other people is the way I wish we ALL could see things: with no artifice, no underlying motivations, and no cruelty. <br><br>And that is how the writing is structured. <br><br>Short, concise paragraphs that are simple in nature but tell a story of great complexity, beauty, and depth. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478103067ra/21032004.gif" width="500" height="213" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, something I am always a sucker for and always will be is the PNR Mate trope.<br><br>Well, this definitely has that, but in a different way than I've ever read before. <br><br>The connection between Ox and all of the other characters is so awesome, so simple, and yet so beautifully complex at the same time. <br><br>They way they all interact and play off each other is alternately heart wrenching, endearing, and hilarious.<br><br>I don't want to talk too much about the story line though because, being that I went in kind of blind myself and loved it, I would encourage others to do so as well. <br> <br>But I will say this...<br><br><b>What this book <i><u>doesn't</u></i> have is:</b><br><br>- A whole lotta steam...nothing really happens between any of the characters until the end. And you know what? I didn't notice the loss...and I'm a huge "I need the sexy times" whore. <br><br>- Artificial drama. So nice. So refreshing. <br><br><b>What this book <i><u>does</u></i> have is:</b><br><br>- Beautiful characters with beautiful connections<br><br>- A love story built over the course of more than a decade<br><br>- Grief and healing<br><br>- Some angst and groveling<br><br>- Camaraderie in spades <br><br>So if any of that cranks your tractor, I say snag this book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478104203ra/21032197.gif" width="500" height="196" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Find this review, other reviews, and general shameless shenanigans at:<br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477498810i/20958471.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477498810i/20958472.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.steamyreads.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477498810i/20958473.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=hype-hype-hype">hype-hype-hype</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=great-chemistry">great-chemistry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=full-of-angst">full-of-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=favorites-2016">favorites-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=losing-the-v-card">losing-the-v-card</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1648615377" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2200710494969134556"><b>PRICE DROP TODAY TO $0.99 AT AMAZON US IF YOU DON'T OWN THIS ONE! 4/4/19</b><br/><br/><i>**Spoiler-free review**</i> <br/><br/>*4.5 stars*<br/><br/><b>RAWR! <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune' title='T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>T.J. Klune</a> writing a shifter book? I'm soooooo there!</b><br/><br/>First of all, I'm a total <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune' title='T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>T.J. Klune</a> fan-girl, so when I saw that he was writing a werewolves book, I just about died. I know what you all want to know: <b>does this book deliver?</b> The answer is <b>YES!</b> Do you also want to know more about the story, the really relevant things, not just a plot summary? If the answer is YES, then read on!<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune' title='T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>T.J</a></span>
  <span id="freeText2200710494969134556" style="display:none"><b>PRICE DROP TODAY TO $0.99 AT AMAZON US IF YOU DON'T OWN THIS ONE! 4/4/19</b><br /><br /><i>**Spoiler-free review**</i> <br /><br />*4.5 stars*<br /><br /><b>RAWR! <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> writing a shifter book? I'm soooooo there!</b><br /><br />First of all, I'm a total <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> fan-girl, so when I saw that he was writing a werewolves book, I just about died. I know what you all want to know: <b>does this book deliver?</b> The answer is <b>YES!</b> Do you also want to know more about the story, the really relevant things, not just a plot summary? If the answer is YES, then read on!<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> has two main writing styles: serious (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30027867.Withered___Sere" title="Withered + Sere by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Withered + Sere</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17213054.Into_This_River_I_Drown" title="Into This River I Drown by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Into This River I Drown</a>) and hilarious (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17194490.Tell_Me_It_s_Real__At_First_Sight___1_" title="Tell Me It's Real (At First Sight, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Tell Me It's Real</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28485201.The_Lightning_Struck_Heart__Tales_From_Verania___1_" title="The Lightning-Struck Heart (Tales From Verania, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lightning-Struck Heart</a>), with some intersection in between (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25548442.How_to_Be_a_Normal_Person__How_to_Be___1_" title="How to Be a Normal Person (How to Be, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">How To Be A Normal Person</a>). <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a> falls squarely in the <b>serious</b> camp, with little moments of levity, but lots and lots of angst. <br /><br />I like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> in all forms of his writing. I like it when he writes his really light-hearted stuff, and I like it when he writes his heart-breaking stuff. This book also had a particular style of writing that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> often uses, mostly with his heavier stuff. There is a lot of repetition of important lines and text, over and over again throughout the story, and a lot of imagery that is very <b>evocative</b> to the reader. The style is also more poetic and less "He went to the store and bought chicken. Then he went to the park." <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> is very deliberate and conscious of his word choice in this story, and it reads more like fantasy than most paranormal/shifter romances that I'm used to. <b>That is a good thing</b>, and I'm always grateful that T.J. shows us different stuff than any other author. <br /><br />This book is also, dare I say it, <b>sexy</b>. T.J. Klune is known to be a lot of things, but a writer of really down and dirty sex scenes... yeah, not his bag. I'm a lover of the sexy parts of romance novels, but I never mind the lack of sex in a T.J. Klune book. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a>, however, was pretty freakin' hot at parts. I mean, we only get a couple of scenes here or there, but I was <b>
  <i>impressed</i>
</b>, man! I think it will be a pleasant surprise for some readers who aren't expecting T.J. to really turn up the heat. <br /><br />What excited me most about this book, however, wasn't the really special writing style or the plot line, which was interesting but not anything particularly mind-blowing in the world of shifter romance. What impressed me was how <b>completely awesome the romance was between Ox and Joe</b>. I swear, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a> can write chemistry like no other. <br /><br />I often struggle with romance books where there is a lot of telling about the connection between two MCs but no showing. SHOW ME THE LOOOOVE. I love an <b>EPIC</b> romance, and so many authors give me a friends-with-benefits vibe. That is NOT a problem in this book. <b>Ox and Joe have a romance for the ages, and <i>not</i> because of some silly shifter-book "insta-love" mates thing, which I see <i>all</i> the time.</b> We really get to see Ox and Joe grow and change together, overcoming insurmountable obstacles, and getting stronger and more complex as a couple. <br /><br />Now, on the topic of Ox and Joe as a couple, I did feel a little like, "wait, haven't I seen this before with a T.J. book?" The big age gap, the crushes, the childhood friends thing. It felt SO familiar. Then I realized what it was: I had been getting a BIG Tyson and Dominic vibe (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20624305.The_Art_of_Breathing__Bear__Otter__and_the_Kid___3_" title="The Art of Breathing (Bear, Otter, and the Kid, #3) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">The Art of Breathing</a>). Now, that isn't a bad thing, even a little bit, but it did feel a little familiar to me and it might also to you.<br /><br />Onto a slightly different topic, there are... things that happen in this book that made me feel VERY frustrated and mad. I was frustrated along with some of the MCs, and one of the things I am most grateful for is that T.J. Klune didn't let ANY characters off the hook easily. It is one of my biggest pet peeves when a character does something that makes me mad, and the other characters just let it go like nothing ever happened, like they weren't ever upset. NO. <b>I LOVE that T.J. let his characters be resentful and petty and frustrated and emotional and annoyed, just like real people.</b> There are a lot of emotions there that really rang true for me. <br /><br />I also <b>loved T.J.'s secondary characters</b>... and there are a LOT of them. In fact, I had a hard time remembering who was who in the beginning. All of those names... it all jumbled together! By the end I had it sorted out, but I was lost for little pieces at the beginning. However, the characters that he does write are very, very strong. They all felt well-rounded, and I have high hopes that a number of them will be getting their own stories in this series in the future. <br /><br />What this book didn't do for me, that it seemed to do with every other reader, was make me cry. I sat there not crying like a callous beotch during some really sad scenes. I'm not sure why I wasn't quite touched on that level... but I wasn't. It isn't a bad thing, especially considering the emotional <i>wrecking</i> that I went through with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28507063.Withered___Sere__Immemorial_Year___1_" title="Withered + Sere (Immemorial Year, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Withered + Sere</a>, but I just wasn't <i>there</i>. Don't get me wrong, I felt a LOT of emotions during this story, but it didn't destroy me. <br /><br />I'm going to wrap this review up, I swear!<br /><br />Basically, all of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5073330.T_J__Klune" title="T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">T.J. Klune</a>'s fans will love this book. <b>It was fabulous and well-written, just like we've all come to expect from T.J., with the added bonus of some sexy-times and some light brushes of humor.</b> I think shifter book fans, and those who have never tried one, will eat this one up, and I know that this series had some AWESOME things in store for us. <br /><br />**Copy provided in exchange for an honest review**</span>
  <a data-text-id="2200710494969134556" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1591300629" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1591300629" />
    <a title="☆ Todd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12415682-todd"><img alt="☆ Todd" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539502816p2/12415682.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1591300629?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Todd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Todd" href="/user/show/12415682-todd">☆ Todd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12415682-todd?shelf=boy-babble">boy-babble</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12415682-todd?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1591300629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15128035043492400594"><br/><b>And that right there, ladies and some more ladies and probably a few gentlemen, is how you write a freaking shifter novel!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/TfBEOKx' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464572032i/19252072._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is the tale of the <b>Bennett pack of werewolf shifters</b>, the oldest, most respected pack in the entire country, and how <b>a human boy named Ox</b> first heals the broken family at the end of the lane and then makes them stronger than they'd ever been before.<br/><br/>At the core of the story, though, are <b>Ox Matheson</b> and <b>Joe Bennett</b>. How they meet, how they grow up, together and separat</span>
  <span id="freeText15128035043492400594" style="display:none"><br><b>And that right there, ladies and some more ladies and probably a few gentlemen, is how you write a freaking shifter novel!</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/TfBEOKx" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464572032i/19252072._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is the tale of the <b>Bennett pack of werewolf shifters</b>, the oldest, most respected pack in the entire country, and how <b>a human boy named Ox</b> first heals the broken family at the end of the lane and then makes them stronger than they'd ever been before.<br><br>At the core of the story, though, are <b>Ox Matheson</b> and <b>Joe Bennett</b>. How they meet, how they grow up, together and separately, how they become family and eventually more. <b>Mates</b>.<br><br>At 12, <b>Ox's</b> drunken father leaves for good, telling his son that he's <b>"<i>dumb as an ox</i>"</b> and that <b>"<i>people will give you shit all your life</i>."</b> Ox never feels like he fits in and that <b>he isn't worth much at all.</b><br><br>Then 4 years later, Ox meets <b>a little blond tornado</b> named <b>Joe</b> on the side of the road, who is convinced that <b>Ox is his personal "<i>everything</i>."</b><br><br>At 10 years old, Joe had been <b>kidnapped and broken by a monster</b>. He'd withdrawn from the world and <b>hadn't spoken a single word for over a year</b>. Until he meets a 16 y.o. boy who immediately becomes his entire world.<br><br>The next 7 years are mostly "<b>
  <i>candy canes and pinecones and epic and awesome</i>
</b>," with lots of humor and touching moments of family and belonging -- until <b>Joe's monster returns</b> and TJ gives us a huge dose of <b>wookie cry face</b>. Bastard.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/dARvWct" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464572363i/19252183.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'll be honest, with as many books as I read, I've gotten <b>fairly desensitized</b> to sad parts in books and often find myself saying, <b>
  <i>"Shouldn't this be making me cry?"</i>
</b> Well, <u>not</u> this time. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>There in the forest, under a new moon and stars that lied, we sang our pack home. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><a href="http://imgur.com/RlsbRhS" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464571878i/19252067._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Yes, I cried.</b> And cried. Then cried some more. Like a goddamn baby.<br><br>However, worse than the aftermath of the attack is <b>the long separation</b> that follows. (<i>This part made me want to punch one T.J. Klune squarely in his junk, guys. Sorry, love you, T.J. heh</i>) <blockquote>
  <b>Three years. <br>One month. <br>Twenty-six days.</b>
</blockquote>That dividing of the pack, and our boys, is awful, but necessary, I suppose. It doesn't mean that I liked it, though.<br><br>During those 3 years, the pack not only heals, mostly, but <b>Ox also comes into his own, becoming what the pack, <i>his pack</i>, needs him to be</b>.<br><br>When Joe finally returns home, <b>Ox is just so very angry</b> that he doesn't know if he'll ever be able to forgive Joe for <b>abandoning him and his family</b> when they all needed him the most.<br><br>But TJ isn't a <i>complete</i> fucker, so past hurts are slowly forgiven and, as expected, <b>Ox and Joe do get their hard-won HEA.</b><br><br>What I truly loved about this book was that, yes, it was a shifter story, but <b>TJ didn't quite adhere to the typical werewolf lore '<i>rules</i>'</b> found in all of the other shifter stories that I've read. <br><br>I was <b>in awe of where TJ took Ox's character</b> and what, as a <i>human</i>, he accomplished for the pack. <b>What he became for the pack, out of necessity. Out of love. And out of loss.</b><br><br>Yes, there were <b>metric tons of angst and tears</b> in this story, but there was <b>so much love, so much connection between the characters</b> that it all felt like <b>a <i>continual</i> lightning strike to the heart</b>. (<i>See what I did there?</i>) ;- )<br><br>The decade-long story just flowed and every single one of the plot points <b>felt natural and entirely essential</b>. There were no drama llamas or contrivances on any of the book's 400 pages.<br><br><b>"Wolfsong" is one of TJ's best works to date and is easily one of my all-time favorite books.</b><br><br>So do not pass go. Do not collect $200. <b>Go directly to "<i>One Click</i>"</b> and get this great <b>4.75 star</b> book ASAP.<br><br>----------------------------------------------<br><br><i>My ARC copy of the book was provided by the publisher in exchange for a fair, unbiased review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="15128035043492400594" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <i>
    <b>He said,"There was never anyone else the entire time I was gone.There was never anyone else for me.Because even if you couldn't hear me when I called for you,the howl in my heart was always meant for you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599711.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599712._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599713._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599714.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599715.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Every once in a while a book comes along that you weren't expecting and just blows you away.<br/>I'd read friends reviews for this and got the sample but the only thing putting me of was that it's quite long and the lack of steam.<br/>Well,I started reading it and right from the first</span>
  <span id="freeText4794329978851244967" style="display:none">5 Stars.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He said,"There was never anyone else the entire time I was gone.There was never anyone else for me.Because even if you couldn't hear me when I called for you,the howl in my heart was always meant for you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599711.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599712._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599713._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599714.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467498434i/19599715.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Every once in a while a book comes along that you weren't expecting and just blows you away.<br>I'd read friends reviews for this and got the sample but the only thing putting me of was that it's quite long and the lack of steam.<br>Well,I started reading it and right from the first page it sucked me in and I was completely captivated by Ox.<br><br>He's 12 when the book opens,a bit of a loner with no self worth.<br>When he's 16 he notices the house down the lane,which has been empty for a while,is now occupied by a family...<br>The Bennett's.<br>One day he meets the youngest,10 year old Joe.A little blonde tornado who rocks into his world and won't let go.Little does Ox know that this meeting will change his life forever....<br><br>I've read a few shifter books but this is in a different league.<br>I loved the characters.<br>I loved the family and feeling of belonging.<br>There's love,loss,deep connections and bonds that are unbreakable.<br><br>It's the first book I've read by this Author and to say I was impressed is an understatement....the writing is simply stunning.<br><br>Just an amazing,emotional story...</span>

<div id="review_1764552178" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1764552178" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1764552178?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Christy by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2016-audios">2016-audios</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1764552178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4509317526232982857"><b> 5 stars!</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/5384874A-81FE-4ABE-A9BD-EF84C2AAB9FB_zpshwcnnrfb.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477388075i/20944233._SX540_.png' alt=' photo 5384874A-81FE-4ABE-A9BD-EF84C2AAB9FB_zpshwcnnrfb.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>So I have a friend who recommended this book to me. I put it on my TBR and said I’d read it soon. Then a few weeks later, she said ‘Hey! Have you read this yet?’ Since I was getting badgered (LOL) I looked it up to see if it was on audible. It was, so I knew it was meant to be. I started listening right away. <i>Wolfsong</i> is a story of family, friendship, loyalty and love. It’s my first read by TJ Klune, but I plan to read many more. Especially if there are spin-offs from this book. I </span>
  <span id="freeText4509317526232982857" style="display:none"><b> 5 stars!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/5384874A-81FE-4ABE-A9BD-EF84C2AAB9FB_zpshwcnnrfb.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477388075i/20944233._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 5384874A-81FE-4ABE-A9BD-EF84C2AAB9FB_zpshwcnnrfb.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So I have a friend who recommended this book to me. I put it on my TBR and said I’d read it soon. Then a few weeks later, she said ‘Hey! Have you read this yet?’ Since I was getting badgered (LOL) I looked it up to see if it was on audible. It was, so I knew it was meant to be. I started listening right away. <i>Wolfsong</i> is a story of family, friendship, loyalty and love. It’s my first read by TJ Klune, but I plan to read many more. Especially if there are spin-offs from this book. I know a few characters that need their own story ;) <br><i>
  <blockquote>“It’s always the ones who are the quietest who often have the greatest things to say.” </blockquote>
</i><br>Ox’s father left him and his mother when he was 12. Ox was always a little on the quiet side. He never really fit in. He started working at a local mechanic’s shop shortly after and found a group there that got him. But it wasn’t until the Bennett’s came into town that he truly felt that sense of family and belonging. On his sixteenth birthday, his life is forever changed when Joe Bennett comes into it. Joe’s family is a little different, but that’s okay with Ox. I love how everyone in this story embraces differences. <br><br>There are some fantastic characters in this story. Not just the main ones, so many of the secondary ones had a place in my heart. Everyone has a purpose to the story. As much as I loved them all, none were as special to me as Ox. I completely adored him. I loved his relationships. His relationship with his mom, with Gordo, all his guys at the shop, and everyone in the Bennett family. His relationship with Joe is by far the most important. I love how it started out as friendship, then grew into so much more. Joe saw Ox as the man he really was. He wasn’t the quiet, awkward boy. He was everything. Sigh. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“You don’t get to decide what you’re worth because you obviously don’t know. You don’t get to decide that anymore because you have no fucking idea that you’re worth everything.”</blockquote>
</i><br>This was a long book, but it didn’t feel long. It was one of those audios that made me want to put down whatever book I was reading so I could focus on listening to it. There were lots of moments I smiled, some moments of laughter, tears, and even frustration. You will get frustrated a time or two, but it’s okay. It’s all okay at the end. The angst was so worth it. <br><br>TJ Klune wrote an outstanding, emotional and extraordinary story when he wrote <i>Wolfsong</i>. I can’t think of one thing I didn’t love about it. The narration was fantastic if you like audio. I highly recommend this one! 5 stars! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I just want to be wherever you are.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/8F7664A5-0B82-4C42-81F0-EDAC834A457D_zpsx7tztp5q.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477388075i/20944234._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 8F7664A5-0B82-4C42-81F0-EDAC834A457D_zpsx7tztp5q.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1779877060" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1779877060" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1779877060?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=mind-fucking-blown">mind-fucking-blown</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying">i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1779877060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2381073780349541591"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497895713i/23067323._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i> “You don’t get to decide what you’re worth because you obviously don’t know. You don’t get to decide that anymore because you have no fucking idea that you’re worth everything.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>How does one review perfection? I don’t know. But I am sure going to try.<br/><br/>I knew from chapter 1 this was going to be a 5 star read. That this was going to be the best thing I've read in a while. Or maybe even one of the best books I've read, <b>EVER.</b><br/><br/>You know when a book is so good you have to go back and re-read chapter</span>
  <span id="freeText2381073780349541591" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497895713i/23067323._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i> “You don’t get to decide what you’re worth because you obviously don’t know. You don’t get to decide that anymore because you have no fucking idea that you’re worth everything.” </i>
</b><br><br>How does one review perfection? I don’t know. But I am sure going to try.<br><br>I knew from chapter 1 this was going to be a 5 star read. That this was going to be the best thing I've read in a while. Or maybe even one of the best books I've read, <b>EVER.</b><br><br>You know when a book is so good you have to go back and re-read chapters because you just don't want it to end? You know when a book is so good that you RUSH home and shut out the world so you can focus on the story and nothing else? You know when a book is so good you sneak your kindle out wherever you are so you can just be with the characters for a little while longer?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482270580i/21500018._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That was this book. In fact, I don't think I'll ever stop reading it. I think I'll just re-read chapters for the rest of time.<br><br><b>
  <i>“And I’ve been waiting,” Joe said. “For him to look at me like I looked at him. And he finally did. He finally did. And I’m going to do everything I can to make sure it stays like that. Because I want him for always.”</i>
</b><br><br>I mean. I highlighted whole chapters. WHOLE ENTIRE FREAKING CHAPTERS.<br><br>I was not prepared for the emotional slaughter this put me through. I was NOT prepared to fall in love with the simplistic writing style. Or to laugh as hard as I did. Or to have my heart burst from the love that oozed from the pages or the incredible characters.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You confuse me. You aggravate me. You’re amazing and beautiful, and sometimes, I want to put my teeth in you just to watch you bleed. I want to know what you taste like. I want to leave my marks on your skin. I want to cover you until all you smell like is me. I don’t want anyone to touch you ever again. I want you. Every part of you.” </i>
</b><br><br>To quote the great <a>Suanne Laqueur</a>, “What the fuck is this book doing being a profoundly beautiful love story?” For real, TJ Klune. Who the hell do you think you are creating this masterpiece?<br><br>Wtf man.<br><br>You’ve ruined me. <b>RUINED ME.</b> You have also sabotaged anything I try and pick up after this. There is no freaking way anything will compare.<br><br>All kidding aside, <u>every single person</u> needs to read this book. I will be harassing you until you do. =D<br><br><b>
  <i>“There was never anyone else the entire time I was gone. There was never anyone else for me. Because even if you couldn’t hear me when I called for you, the howl in my heart was always meant for you.” </i>
</b><br><br>Wolfsong | <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://amzn.to/2oU9Bys">https://amzn.to/2oU9Bys</a><br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Find Me On:<br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thecrazyworldofabooklover/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=100009277089211" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Page</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2102996313?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="chan ☆" class="user" itemprop="url" name="chan ☆" href="/user/show/48727754-chan">chan ☆</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=lgbtq">lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=all-time-faves">all-time-faves</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2102996313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18052655571791486467"><b>imagine if Bella didn’t suck and had chosen the werewolves and was also gay</b><br/><br/>this book follows Ox Matheson as he navigates life and growing up in a small town. at the beginning of the novel we see his father leave and a new family move in "down the lane" which really starts the beginning of Ox's life. <br/><br/>i can't do justice to this story or the way it was written, honestly. this book spans a nearly 10 year period and is told exclusively through Ox's point of view. his relationships both familial and r</span>
  <span id="freeText18052655571791486467" style="display:none"><b>imagine if Bella didn’t suck and had chosen the werewolves and was also gay</b><br /><br />this book follows Ox Matheson as he navigates life and growing up in a small town. at the beginning of the novel we see his father leave and a new family move in "down the lane" which really starts the beginning of Ox's life. <br /><br />i can't do justice to this story or the way it was written, honestly. this book spans a nearly 10 year period and is told exclusively through Ox's point of view. his relationships both familial and romantic are so full of heart and so damn real that you often forget you're reading a shifter/paranormal book. there's violence and drama too but this book shines so bright in its depiction of relationships.<br /><br />also the INTENSE character development of the two main men in this book is so gradual and yet so perfect. i love seeing confidence being built after traumatic experiences and this book does such a realistic job at exploring that.<br /><br />i always fell DEEPLY in love with the way this was written. we're inside Ox's head the entire time and we actually see his character development through the writing. he goes from quiet and unsure to complicated and well spoken. the writing is ADDICTING. beautiful in its simplicity and so unputdownable. <br /><br />oh also i actually LOLed reading this, often????<br /><br />please go pick this up if you're looking for a family centric, HEART WARMING AF romance. even if you're skeptical of paranormal.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=2019-challenge">2019-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1647296929" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10983506877975638061">5 Stars! <br/><br/>Re-read 7-11-18<br/><br/>Second time around and it was just as enthralling and brilliant as the first time. This is a story you can't help but get sucked into never wanting to leave these characters behind. I can not wait for the next book! xx<br/>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br/>What can I say... TJ... You blew my mind once again. <br/><br/>I cannot say enough how much I <b>LOVE</b> this mans writing. The worlds and characters he creates are nothing if not brilliant. The way he weaves a story together whil</span>
  <span id="freeText10983506877975638061" style="display:none">5 Stars! <br /><br />Re-read 7-11-18<br /><br />Second time around and it was just as enthralling and brilliant as the first time. This is a story you can't help but get sucked into never wanting to leave these characters behind. I can not wait for the next book! xx<br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br />What can I say... TJ... You blew my mind once again. <br /><br />I cannot say enough how much I <b>LOVE</b> this mans writing. The worlds and characters he creates are nothing if not brilliant. The way he weaves a story together while at the same time managing to create so many different characters who are so unique in their own right in <b>ONE</b> book has me in awe of him. Whenever I see a new book coming out by this guy it's an automatic buy for me. He's a go to read. He's unique in what he writes. He has a way of grabbing you and keeping hold of you throughout his stories that you don't feel the number of pages you read. You don't miss the sex you get in so many other books. He captures you by his unique story telling and his amazing characters he has created. The guy is brilliant and so was this story.<br /><br />I waited awhile to read this one. I needed the hype and all the posting of it to slow down before I could start it. It was hard because so many were reading it and posting amazing reviews or comments on it, but I held out. Until I couldn't anymore. <br /><br />Once I started this I couldn't put it down. It, like so many of T.J.'s books, grabbed me and wouldn't let me go. I was completely useless to my family while reading this and annoyed them greatly as they did me when they tried to interrupt my reading. LOL<br /><br />Ox. What a special character. I adored him. He was so damn sweet. He's 12 when the story begins and I loved that we got to grow with him. He is a character that will capture your heart. He did mine and by the end I was completely in love with this character. <br /><br />Once the Bennett's show up everything gets more interesting. The family is close and I loved them all. Especially the twins and of course, Joe. He was just too cute. The friendship between him and Ox was so damn adorable. <br /><br />Joe and Ox's story starts when they're both kids. Ox being 16 and Joe being 10. They meet as Ox is walking home. Joe is standing in the middle of the dirt road and tells Ox that he smells of, <b> candy canes and pinecones and epic and awesome</b>. And their relationship blooms from there. We watch them grow, separate, and come back together. <br /><br />I don't want to give much of the story away. Just know it's amazing and just writing this review makes me want to read it all over again.<br /><br />I recommend this one to everyone. Even if this isn't your type of read, try it. The characters, writing, and story building is too great to miss out on. Enjoy, dolls! xx</span>

  This is by far one of the best shifter books, I have ever read !!

I also don't want to spoiler.<br/><br/>The only thing you'll need to know, is that this book is about <strong>candy canes and pinecones</strong> and <strong>epic and awesome</strong> !!!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495616170i/22836466.jpg' alt='photo christmas-decorations-top-view-candy-canes-composition-cones-linen-fabric-background-63332161_zpsu4r0ff5m.jpg: ' width='288' height='191' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book gave me so much. It made me <strong>smile</strong>, <strong>cry</strong>, <strong>swoon</strong> and <strong>laugh out loud</strong>. It had me on the edge of my seat, and once I started it, there was no stopping. My emotions were all ove</span>
  <span id="freeText15712950277728898535" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1490384633i/22308885._SX540_.jpg" alt="five-star-client.png (822Ã—172): " width="263" height="55" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>
  This is by far one of the best shifter books, I have ever read !!
</p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495616170ra/22836465.gif" alt="totally-awesome.gif (361Ã—339)" width="210" height="197" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm not going into the plot or anything, because I couldn't even explain the awesomeness, that is this book. I also don't want to spoiler.<br><br>The only thing you'll need to know, is that this book is about <strong>candy canes and pinecones</strong> and <strong>epic and awesome</strong> !!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495616170i/22836466.jpg" alt="photo christmas-decorations-top-view-candy-canes-composition-cones-linen-fabric-background-63332161_zpsu4r0ff5m.jpg: " width="288" height="191" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book gave me so much. My emotions were all over the place...but in a good way.<br><br>I loved every single character in this book !! That doesn't happen very often. At the end, they all felt like my family....oh how I wish ;) <br><br>It's about a <strong>family of wolf-shifters</strong> and <strong>a human boy</strong>, who is so much more than he ever thought he would be. It's about <strong>pack</strong> and <strong>unconditional love</strong>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495616170i/22836467.jpg" alt="decd6182df0daf1cda53d69edf198da2.jpg (236Ã—254): " width="205" height="221" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's about loss and finding out who you truly are, and where you belong. It's about Ox and Joe, two of the most <strong>wonderfull characters</strong> ever !!<br><br>
  <strong><em>“We're friends first,” Joe whispered in my ear. “You’re my best friend, Ox, and I promise that will never change. We’ll just be… more.”</em> </strong>

  <br>
  I would recommend this one, to everyone who loves a good shifter book, because this one definitely deserves 6 stars !!!

<div id="review_1648308455" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1648308455" />
    <a title="Sheziss" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7547092-sheziss"><img alt="Sheziss" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1461185007p2/7547092.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1648308455?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sheziss" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sheziss" href="/user/show/7547092-sheziss">Sheziss</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=2000s">2000s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=tortured-souls">tortured-souls</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=wonderful-narrator">wonderful-narrator</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=against-all-odds-there-is-hope">against-all-odds-there-is-hope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=i-love-you-in-silence">i-love-you-in-silence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=bmbr">bmbr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=different-species">different-species</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7547092-sheziss?shelf=dreamspinner-press">dreamspinner-press</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1648308455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13155280057924128593"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465549556i/19371400._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This smells of pinecones and candy canes. Of epic and awesome.<br/><br/>I don’t exactly remember the smell of pinecones and candy cones right now.<br/><br/>But I will always remember the smell of epic and awesome.<br/><br/>It’s a power some have. A power a few people on Earth simply have. The power of writing epic and awesome. The power of creating epic and awesome.<br/><br/>This is an epic and awesome creation. And it’s powerful. In every sense of the word.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466074711i/19435657.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I loved everything in this book. I loved Ox. I loved Joe. I loved the pack, as</span>
  <span id="freeText13155280057924128593" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465549556i/19371400._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This smells of pinecones and candy canes. Of epic and awesome.<br><br>I don’t exactly remember the smell of pinecones and candy cones right now.<br><br>But I will always remember the smell of epic and awesome.<br><br>It’s a power some have. A power a few people on Earth simply have. The power of writing epic and awesome. The power of creating epic and awesome.<br><br>This is an epic and awesome creation. And it’s powerful. In every sense of the word.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466074711i/19435657.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved everything in this book. I loved Ox. I loved Joe. I loved the pack, as a whole, and each one of them individually. I loved the family. I loved the friends. I loved the bonds. I loved the sexy. I loved the kink (yes, the KINK). I loved the fluffy. I loved the rawness. I loved the laughs. I loved the lump in my throat. I loved the magic. I loved the wolves. I loved the sense of belonging. The sense of ownership. The sense of conquering. The sense of surrendering. The sense of acknowledge. The sense of goodbye. The sense of marking. The sense of mating. The sense of despair. The sense of exhilaration. The sense of completion. The sense of perfection.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466074083i/19435442.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was poetry in prose. This inner voice. This earthy voice. This mystical voice. This soundless voice. A voice that reverberates. A voice that pulls you under. A voice that makes you fly. It was an insistent voice, an evocative voice, a tactile voice. Pictures behind my eyelids. Vibrations inside my bones. Sinking feeling in my stomach. It’s a voice that surrounds everything and impregnates everything. It’s a voice I can touch and I can caress. It’s a voice that touches and caresses me. From the inside. It’s warmth and it’s love. It was liquid and solid. Without defined shape. Without defined color. It’s powerful. <br><br>Violet, blue, red, orange. Green.<br><br>Green. Green. Green.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465736015i/19394865.jpg" width="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>I felt I was dying and seeing the sun for the first time in my life. <br><br>I felt I was flying too close to the sun. <br><br>I felt I was touching this sun and setting myself afire.<br><br>Once and again. <br><br>Once and again. <br><br>And again.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466073869i/19435332._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some books don’t exist but there is always a place waiting for them. There was an empty space once. This space screamed. For a long time. Demanding attention. Demanding plenitude. Nobody heard that scream. It existed once. Not anymore. Because this book was created and it filled that space. At last. It was meant to be.<br> <br>What’s this, really? A shifters book? A love story? A tale of family and union? A coming-of-age book? A soul mates’ destiny? A fantasy novel? The light against the dark?<br><br>I don’t dare to say what this is.<br><br>I was so satisfied.<br><br>With everything.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466074189i/19435470._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I marvelled at the long arguments. How things were not black and white. Were not easy to solve. Were not something that could be fixed with a kiss and a few words. I loved the complex conversations. I marvelled at the big mistakes and at the big wise moves. I marvelled at the suffering and the healing. I marvelled at all the hilarious in here. I marvelled at brothership and friendship and “packship” and all the “ships” in the universe.<br><br>I marvelled at a witch working in a garage. I marvelled at Bennet’s pups protecting Ox at school. I marvelled at Ox’s mother kicking like a bad-ass. Rico’s Spanish. Elizabeth’s dances at a song of those who stay behind. Or are left behind. Small displays of genius that are subtle but constant. I’m sure I didn’t catch them all with my conscious mind and that’s why I will never be able to write them and pay a proper homage to them. But deep inside, I saw them all. They were there. I can simply sum it up saying how marvelled I was at the affection I felt for everybody here, because every detail is essential, every little word, every casual scene. Each one of them was carved on stone. Every one of them is there for something. Every breath of theirs is useful and noticeable. The characters not only keep their seats warm, but you feel the lost of warmth when they disappear, and you feel the warmth when they come back. Or the eternal loss when they never do.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466073869ra/19435330.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I marvelled at Ox. <br><br>OxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOxOx. <br><br>His selflessness. His loneliness. His longing. His ability to love. And forgive. And love again. His innocence. His strength. His resilience. His sense of what’s right and what’s wrong. His straightforwardness. His raw honesty. His hesitant self-worth. His large presence. Large as life. His heart on his sleeve but also his guts, his balls. And his brains. Life is going to give him shit, but he will always be standing. <br><br>I love Ox’s love.<br><br>Joe.<br><br>This little tornado who came out nothing. Whose words meant the beginning of it all. Of adventure. Of happiness. Of loss. Of everything. It was simply right that he pronounced those exact words to that exact person in that each moment in that exact place. It was <i>right</i>. His joy. His euphoria. His instincts. His choices, bad and good. His hopelessness. His nightmares. His shadows. His dark. This yearning that makes him tremble. His lack of voice. His trigger to make him talk.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466073869ra/19435331.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The characters were not perfect but they were born that way. Epic and awesome in their own way. Little shining stars in this infinite universe of Klune.<br><br>The story line not only makes sense but feels right. In every moment of the road.<br><br>It’s complex and could go on and on and on. Beyond the ending, there is a “to be continued”. <br><br>An “Hasta la vista, baby”.<br><br>Not exactly an “I will be back” but an “I never left”.<br><br>It’s full of green.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465735128i/19394759.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I was little I wanted to go to Hogwarts. But when I graduate there, I want to move to Green Creek and become part of the Bennet pack.<br><br>*****<br><br>More pics...<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[

<div id="review_1726043504" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1726043504" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1726043504?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=witches-wizards">witches-wizards</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=wolves-lycans">wolves-lycans</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1726043504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17401682899619435471">Men don’t cry! Ox’s dad taught him that. <br/><br/>Well Ox cried a lot. <br/><br/>He cried during sad moments: when he was twelve and his dad abandoned him and his mother.<br/><br/>He cried during happy moments: when he was fifteen and he got a shirt for present. A shirt that signified that he was now part of the Gordo’s team at the shop where he was working.<br/><br/>And he kept crying when he felt like it until he became twenty-five and he stopped sharing his story with us and the book finished. <br/><br/>It seems he had disappointed his fath</span>
  <span id="freeText17401682899619435471" style="display:none">Men don’t cry! Ox’s dad taught him that. <br /><br />Well Ox cried a lot. <br /><br />He cried during sad moments: when he was twelve and his dad abandoned him and his mother.<br /><br />He cried during happy moments: when he was fifteen and he got a shirt for present. A shirt that signified that he was now part of the Gordo’s team at the shop where he was working.<br /><br />And he kept crying when he felt like it until he became twenty-five and he stopped sharing his story with us and the book finished. <br /><br />It seems he had disappointed his father. According to him, Ox did not manage to become a real man. Well f@ck the sperm donor, because he was a looser and an @shhole. He made Ox think that he was not smart, did not deserve anything and was gonna get sh!t for most of his life.<br /><br />I was crying when Ox was crying. And I was also crying when he tried not to cry.<br /><br />Ox did not become the man his father wanted him to be. He became more. Much more. <br /><br />He started as a shy, lonely boy who did not talk much, who barely succeeded in school, who was working at a garage to support his mother.<br /><br />He ended up realizing what he truly was: a leader, a lover, a brother, a son, a friend.<br /><br />When he was sixteen, he gave his heart to a blue eyed boy who loved him and later on he trusted him enough to keep his family safe. <br /><br />Joe was so enchanted with Ox. When he met him, you see, magic happened:<br /> <br />Rawr and grr and kaboom....<br />Candy canes and pinecones and epic and awesome...<br /><br />So Joe gave Ox his stone wolf and he took him to meet his family. A weird family who lived at the house at the end of the lane. And like most of the families, the Bennetts had their own secrets. <br /><br />Soon Ox became part of the Bennetts family. He was <br /><br />running with wolves<br />dancing with wolves<br />singing with wolves<br /><br />Ox had layers, you see, and depth. His story may have started being simple, but it gradually became more complicated. He may have been human, but he was also more. Much more.<br /><br />It did not matter what he thought of himself: “I am Ox. Just Ox. That’s all.”<br />Soon he did what he had to do and he had become what he was supposed to become. <br />Because the world is full of monsters and magic, you see. And Ox had to make choices.<br /><br />The author’s style is almost poetic. Like Ox is whispering and singing lyrics to the readers. Stories about how he grew up, how he fell in love. His pack story. His life story. <br /><br />The whole book is a song. You may thing you are reading a novel, but you will be reading poetry. <br />Absolutely fantastic! Absolutely inspiring!<br /><br />It is by far the best book that I have read this year and one of the best books about shifters I have ever read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17401682899619435471" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2250575581" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2241838868491393045"><b>look I really wanted to like this</b> it has such a high rating on goodreads and all my friends gave it five stars and I HONESTLY thought it would be a five star read for me but, alas. I probably would have dnf'ed this if I didn't need it for Magical Readathon <br/><br/><u>what didn't work</u><br/><br/>	• never got over how icky I felt over the age gap. When the characters meet they're 11 and 16, and from that first meeting they're 'destined' to be mates. Even though they don't start dating until their 17 and 23 (which I stil</span>
  <span id="freeText2241838868491393045" style="display:none"><b>look I really wanted to like this</b> it has such a high rating on goodreads and all my friends gave it five stars and I HONESTLY thought it would be a five star read for me but, alas. I probably would have dnf'ed this if I didn't need it for Magical Readathon <br /><br /><u>what didn't work</u><br /><br />	• never got over how icky I felt over the age gap. When the characters meet they're 11 and 16, and from that first meeting they're 'destined' to be mates. Even though they don't start dating until their 17 and 23 (which I still think is weird lol) it just didn't sit right. ESPECIALLY since a large portion of the 'angst' from the first half is the 11-13 year old being upset the 16-18 year old is dating people who aren't him.... and honestly even when they're adult I still found the whole "you've always been mine since I was ten" WEIRD not CUTE<br /><br />	• as a result never invested in the main couple and investing in the main couple really is 90% of the point of this book<br /><br />	• Couldn't get into the writing. Some people said they found it lyrical but I just found a lot of it corny and overly repetitive. The humour also wasn't my kind of humour so the funny parts sometimes read cringy to me<br /><br />	• all the women characters exist to be fridged for the male angst/pain or to be emotional soundboards with no personality except to soothe and console the men when they feel angsty and need advice <br /><br />	• honestly just found the story boring and the plot doesn't even kick in till well over 50% through<br /><br /><u>what I did like</u><br /><br />	• good casual representation I LOVE how everyone is queer and all the queer relationships we get and how normal and chill it is. ownvoices representation<br />	• the found family elements and the focus on the love between family and friends<br />	• my boy carter<br />	• reminded me of a teen wolf episode<br /><br />Honestly <b>it's probably me not this book</b> because it has a 4.5 rating but urgh, sadly this just did not work for me</span>

<div id="review_2093873000" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2093873000" />
    <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner"><img alt="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532688964p2/31461418.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2093873000?book_show_action=true">Aug 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>
