          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=trigger-warning">trigger-warning</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>,

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2093873000" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16273278757027918011"><b>EDIT 08/02/2018</b> : First of all, I won't delete this review. It seems important to me to keep it, because I stand by what I said the first time : ultimately, Joe's parents were abusive. They didn't give Ox a choice. It will never be okay. As much as I can, now, find it in me to accept it, rather than love it, I'm not disowning myself. But. I just read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35114241.Ravensong__Green_Creek___2_' title='Ravensong (Green Creek, #2) by T.J. Klune' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ravensong</a> and <i>the weirdest thing happened</i> : <b>I fell in love with these characters again</b>. Because perhaps my review didn't make it clear then, but I </span>
  <span id="freeText16273278757027918011" style="display:none"><b>EDIT 08/02/2018</b> : First of all, I won't delete this review. It seems important to me to keep it, because I stand by what I said the first time : ultimately, Joe's parents were abusive. They didn't give Ox a choice. It will never be okay. As much as I can, now, find it in me to accept it, rather than love it, I'm not disowning myself. But. I just read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35114241.Ravensong__Green_Creek___2_" title="Ravensong (Green Creek, #2) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Ravensong</a> and <i>the weirdest thing happened</i> : <b>I fell in love with these characters again</b>. Because perhaps my review didn't make it clear then, but I did love them. It hurt <i>because</i> I did love them. In the end, I don't know if <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35114241.Ravensong__Green_Creek___2_" title="Ravensong (Green Creek, #2) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Ravensong</a> mended my heart or if I just needed to wait a year to reread <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a>, even though there are parts of it I'm not able to reread and probably never will, I just know that the moment Gordo expressed my feelings in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35114241.Ravensong__Green_Creek___2_" title="Ravensong (Green Creek, #2) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Ravensong</a>? I <i>cried</i>, because thank you thank you someone <i>saw it.</i> It doesn't make it okay, but I care so much, I know I won't be able to stay away from the rest of the series and it would feel dishonest not to tell you. Oh, and. I deleted my rating because I really do not know what to make of it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1502900506i/23608763._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a> hurt me. Not for the reasons I thought it would but it hurt me it hurt me <i>it hurt me.</i> I've been reading it all day, I did, all the over-winded hundreds of pages of it, I've been reading all day and I couldn't shut out the voices that said <i>would you stop this is abusive stop stop no don't you dare caring no this is abuse this is abuse this is abuse.</i><br><br>In the end, I probably needed this reminder : <b>an abusive relationship is not always something that you can reject instantly because it doesn't stink of evilness and wrongness - even though parts of you <i>know</i> - but looks so much like love and tenderness and appeals to everything in us that screams <i>please need me</i></b>. Over the past years, I've read so many books that pulled these strings and I <i>tore them apart</i>, so much that I trusted myself enough to never fall into such trap again. <br><br>I was wrong. <br><br>Because sometimes, sometimes an author is skilled enough to avoid our wards and confuse us and make us feel that we're wrong, we should root for them, stop thinking, accept accept accept would you just accept their love just do it do it now would you. <br><br><b>I can't, though.</b> If I said that I probably needed this reminder, that's because abuse is not always straightforward. An abusive character is not always someone I hate but one I LOVE and I'm <i>manipulated</i> into loving him <i>so much</i> and here's the hate I was waiting for. Joe. <b>Joe is abusive. There is so much emotional abuse in his relationship with Ox that I want to <i>throw up</i>.</b> Even more because everything in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a> tricks the reader into thinking that it's okay, that codependency is okay, that it's healthy to need someone to fix ourselves but <i>it's not</i>, it fucking isn't, and in the end I feel so damn sad and pissed off and <br><br>m a n i p u l a t e d <br><br>it makes me want to vomit. I want to <i>vomit</i> because I liked both guys and hated them so much. They broke my heart. I loathed that they kept coming at me, tearing up my wards and putting in my mind that it was <i>okay</i> and that <i>I</i> had a problem or wasn't open-minded enough to accept their love but ultimately, that's the thing, see? <b>This is not love, this is fascination and control and this reeks of double standard because I would have raged earlier if one of them had been a woman and <i>what is this bullshit, Anna? Fuck you, Anna.</i> Why should I accept this <i>mine mine mine</i> rhetoric when it's m/m if I wouldn't have if it was a m/f romance?</b> Ugh. Double-standards <i>suck</i>. I know that men can be abused as much as women and I sure know I <i>knew that</i> but it still disgusts me to realize that I was so long to call it out? <br><br>It doesn't help that the story dragged so much and that the events happening in the middle were so <i>useless</i> and over-dramatic and nonsensical and why are you doing this it doesn't make any sense just <i>stop</i>. It doesn't help either that I didn't care for the side characters <i>at all</i> after this point, especially Robbie and Jessie and Tanner and Rico and ugh I don't care okay? I just don't. Shut the fuck <i>up.</i> It doesn't help that the characterization was all over the place and that I don't know what to make of Ox, in the end. It doesn't help, too, that the writing was so so so repetitive (but not devoid of beautiful and wonderful and emotional parts and that's part of why I can't go with 1 star.) (also Joe. Damn it, Joe. I know you don't realize how fucked-up everything is but it doesn't change a thing does it because see, <i>I</i> do.)<br><br>It doesn't help but that's not why I'm going with two stars and I just itch - I itch to give it one star because in the end, <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a> is nothing more than a Twilight rollercoaster of <i>chosen one</i>, codependent, unhealthy relationships, TSTL moments when you don't even know why the characters are so fucking eager to sacrifice themselves for no reasons, I'm sorry, no reasons, with a villain who just cannot fucking <i>die</i> - who is he, seriously? a Terminator phoenix?</b><br><br>And as I got the appeal of Twilight, I understand why people love <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a>. I understand why people adore Joe, god, <i>Joe. </i> It's so easy to but I cannot. <b>I couldn't.</b> Came the end, I was shaking with anger and snarling, oh my god, I was snarling <i>so bad</i>. I might have felt for Ox and Joe, they weren't beautiful together. I said that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29233804.Wolfsong__Green_Creek___1_" title="Wolfsong (Green Creek, #1) by T.J. Klune" rel="nofollow noopener">Wolfsong</a> tricked me, but from the moment I opened my eyes on its flaws, I couldn't look away. And that's just right, because that's what happens with any abusive relationship. <b>Once you see things how they really are, you can't ignore it.</b> Right now, I can't ignore that I wish I hadn't read this book and that I'll never read the words <i>mate</i> and <i>need</i> and <i>only you can fix me</i> again. <br><br><b>My skin crawls, and that's not something I want to feel ever again.</b><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="16273278757027918011" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

You don’t get to decide that anymore because you have no fucking idea that you’re worth everything.” ​ </i> </b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474492697ra/20607483.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>​<br/><br/><br/>This book. THIS BOOK. If I could use the praise hands emoji I would. <b> THIS IS MY FAVORITE BOOK OF 2016 TO DATE! </b> Oh my god, the everloving feels.   <span id="freeText6389578616163893897" style="display:none"><i> ON SALE FOR $1.99!!! <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2txcXrU">http://amzn.to/2txcXrU</a><br>7/1/17 </i><br><br><b> ALL THE STARS! </b><br><br><b> <i> “You don’t get to decide what you’re worth because you obviously don’t know. You don’t get to decide that anymore because you have no fucking idea that you’re worth everything.” ​ </i> </b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474492697ra/20607483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">​<br><br><br>This book. THIS BOOK. If I could use the praise hands emoji I would. <b> THIS IS MY FAVORITE BOOK OF 2016 TO DATE! </b> Oh my god, the everloving feels. This book made my soul hurt, in a good way.<br><br>This book is the story of Ox and Joe. Ox's dad left when he was twelve, leaving Ox feeling worthless and alone. It isn't easy for him to form his thoughts into words, and at school he is mocked for his slowness and treated unkindly. Then when he is sixteen, one day on the way home he runs into a boy who latched onto him and would not stop talking, who took Ox home to his family and they accepted Ox as their own. Ox finally had a family, and the Bennett's embraced him and his mother. Years later, Ox discovers their secret and it opens up his world to new possibilities.<br><br>I don't want to say more than that, because even though it's all in the blurb it feels a bit spoilerly. This book exceeded my expectations and more, it holds a grip on my heart and I won't ever forget this story. Sidenote, thank you to the awesome Eva, a real life friend of mine who never stopped recommending this book to me, I would have never read it otherwise and that would have been a tragedy.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458616698i/18508485.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> “I needed to see him. To make sure he was okay. To tell him how sorry I was. That I never wanted to leave him. That I never wanted to be anywhere but by his side. All I ever wanted was to keep him safe. Ever since that first day on the road, when he spoke and moved like a little tornado, all I ever wanted was to make sure nothing ever happened to Joe Bennett." </i> </b><br><br>Klune has such a poetic writing style, the words flowed across the page and the fluidity of them matched the tone of the novel. My heart broke for Ox, for all of this insecurities and hardships. I loved that sometimes he was blind to what was in front of him when it was staring him in the face. His relationship with Ox, pre-romance and once they were together was stunning, the two of them together just fit perfectly, like puzzle pieces coming together.<br><br>There are so many layers to this story, I honestly could go back and reread it from the beginning again. The side characters, perfection. I really hope there are more books about them whether it is MM or MF because I need to have more of this world in my life!!! Gosh I almost forgot about the world building!! Two thumbs up! Completely believable shifter community, the town, all of it. <br><br>If you've read my ramblings this far, you can tell I just completely fell in love with this book, this story. If you read MM romance, read it now. If you've never read MM make this your first. This is a special story, one that will stay with me a long time.<br><br><b> <i> “I just want to be wherever you are.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455783307i/18148833._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1796477822" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1796477822" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1796477822?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/30853358-wolfsong">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=different">different</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=intrigue">intrigue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=best-of-the-bestest">best-of-the-bestest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=para-fantasy">para-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=the-good-guy-hero">the-good-guy-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=there-will-be-blood">there-will-be-blood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=favourites-2016">favourites-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=m-m-and-m-f-m-and-m-m-f">m-m-and-m-f-m-and-m-m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1796477822" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5911890947484692101"><b>If I could convince you to try, <i>Wolfsong</i> would be the one.</b><br/><br/>My hubby hates coffee and salad. Now, to me, this is WEIRD. How can he survive without coffee? What could he find fault within a nice fresh crisp salad? Every time I have an extraordinary coffee or salad, I say the same thing to him - <i>If I could convert you, THIS will be the one…</i> My poor darling hubby then shakes his head at me, girds his loins and takes a sip or a bite. Now, even weirder…he hates the smell of coffee. So the first problem</span>
  <span id="freeText5911890947484692101" style="display:none"><b>If I could convince you to try, <i>Wolfsong</i> would be the one.</b><br><br>My hubby hates coffee and salad. Now, to me, this is WEIRD. How can he survive without coffee? What could he find fault within a nice fresh crisp salad? Every time I have an extraordinary coffee or salad, I say the same thing to him - <i>If I could convert you, THIS will be the one…</i> My poor darling hubby then shakes his head at me, girds his loins and takes a sip or a bite. Now, even weirder…he hates the smell of coffee. So the first problem is that he’s already scrunching his face up bringing the cup to his mouth. Then, he takes a sip and proceeds to shudder shake and groan. When it comes to the salad, he always says (without fail) - <i>Rabbits food…</i> and grimaces as he swallows. Not once has he said –<i>Baby, that’s not too bad</i>. <br><br>Of course, I’m off track AGAIN!! But, I honestly believe that this is a story that if I could convince you to try paranormal or M/M, <i>Wolfsong</i> would be the one.<br><br>What an adventure. I have experienced every single emotion in <i>Wolfsong</i>. This is the sort of story where you need to find a quiet little corner, shut out your world and escape to another. When I went to this world, I didn’t expect to have my eyes leak for the first 10%. I hardly thought that I would want to jump into the pages to protect a little boy from hurtful words. I never expected to feel jealous of these characters that freely touched, held and cuddled with each other. There was no shame in affection shown in a way that has become foreign to a lot of people, including me. Wouldn’t it be wonderful to, without hesitation, hug someone who needs a hug? Or reach out to someone when you need affection? <br><br>I was truly gobsmacked that for the FIRST TIME EVER, I felt that the sexy scenes weren’t needed to see the connection between the two main characters. I have NEVER felt that way. There was nothing wrong with these scenes. They still made my heart beat faster and my skin flush, but I skimmed over it dying to get to the rest of the story. Wow!! Will wonders never cease?<br><br>There is something awesome about <i>Wolfsong</i> that makes you feel the thread connecting you to the other members in the pack. You feel the tug of the line calling you to be in touching distance with your fellow pack members. You’re ready to stand by your Alpha when the baddies come to attack. I became Bennett Pack and my home was Green Creek.<br><br>It’s not often that I come across a story that grips me as well as <i>Wolfsong</i> did. The characters, the emotions and the storyline were so consuming that I felt moved. I was fortunate enough that a very good book friend of mine pressured me with side-eye glares to just do it. I was tempted to take a chance, step into an unfamiliar world and experience the magic of Wolfsong.<br><br>I haven’t gone into as much detail in this review as I normally would. If you are willing to take a chance, you need to meet the Bennett’s, the townsfolk of Green Creek and the other characters for yourself. If you’re uncertain about reading a paranormal but you love adventure and excitement then this will be a good one to, (maybe) convert you. Uncertain how you would feel about reading an M/M, then this might be the one for you. The intimate scenes are not fleshed out until near the end of the book. <br><br>I loved <i>Wolfsong</i>. <br><br>I was extremely moved by the emotions. <br><br>I have never felt so connected to a story that I felt like I was part of the pack, a member, one of the team. <br><br>I'm convinced that 2016 is the year of <b>The Book Buzz</b>.<br><br>Look, if I could convince you to try, <i>Wolfsong</i> would be the one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1548709401i/26982519.jpg" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5911890947484692101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1633830351" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15461966096192228985"><b>We sort of Gang Banged TJ. His book, I mean! #awkward Check out all the awesome reviews of a book that's sure to make a lot of 2016 Best Of lists!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s356.photobucket.com/user/jackfordandsons/media/b57fbafe-cdb9-4cea-81a4-d8e101acd94c_560_420_zpsprmvt1x0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465960861i/19420895._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo b57fbafe-cdb9-4cea-81a4-d8e101acd94c_560_420_zpsprmvt1x0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I wish I had the words to adequately explain just how much I loved this book. Right from the start 12 yr old Ox grabbed hold of my heart and he's yet to let go. And I loved it. He squeezed it so tight sometimes it made my face leak. And I loved that too. I wish I could smell him like Joe can. I wish I could smell the epic and the awesome and the ca</span>
  <span id="freeText15461966096192228985" style="display:none"><b>We sort of Gang Banged TJ. His book, I mean! #awkward Check out all the awesome reviews of a book that's sure to make a lot of 2016 Best Of lists!</b><br><br><a href="http://s356.photobucket.com/user/jackfordandsons/media/b57fbafe-cdb9-4cea-81a4-d8e101acd94c_560_420_zpsprmvt1x0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465960861i/19420895._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo b57fbafe-cdb9-4cea-81a4-d8e101acd94c_560_420_zpsprmvt1x0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I wish I had the words to adequately explain just how much I loved this book. Right from the start 12 yr old Ox grabbed hold of my heart and he's yet to let go. And I loved it. He squeezed it so tight sometimes it made my face leak. And I loved that too. I wish I could smell him like Joe can. I wish I could smell the epic and the awesome and the candy canes and pinecones all smashed up together. <br><br><a href="http://s356.photobucket.com/user/jackfordandsons/media/Wolf-and-Moon-Cool-HD-Wallpapers_zpszakugkyw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465960861i/19420896._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Wolf-and-Moon-Cool-HD-Wallpapers_zpszakugkyw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even though I can’t have that I will <i>
  <b>always</b>
</i> have Ox. When I’ve had a horrific day and I want everyone to run backwards through a field of dicks. When I start believing the human race incapable of kindness. When I feel my hope faltering. I’ll have Ox. Ox will remind me there is some goodness, innocence and purity left in the world. As will Joe and the rest of the pack.<br><br>This is my first Klune so I’ve no way of knowing whether or not this is representative of his work, but I can say I’ve never read anything like this before. <i>Wolfsong</i> is about family and sacrifice, duty and honor, love and loss, first and forever love, grief and recovery, vengeance and priorities, good versus evil and choice. And how those choices affect those around us and the consequences of those choices. And forgiveness.<br><br><a href="http://s356.photobucket.com/user/jackfordandsons/media/black-and-white-wolf_zps3kmy4rwn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465960861i/19420897._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo black-and-white-wolf_zps3kmy4rwn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I highlighted and bookmarked so much and once I finished it I wanted to go right back to the beginning and get on the ride again. It was the shortest 400 pg book I've ever read. It may have been a little repetitive and maybe some could’ve been edited out, but it was perfect to me and those things are what make Ox… Ox. <br><br>As perfect and poignant as I found <i>Wolfsong</i> to be, I’d be remiss if I didn’t say that if there’s not a follow up I may die. If that's not a recommendation I don't know what is.<br><br><a href="http://boymeetsboyreviews.blogspot.com/2016/06/group-review-wolfsong-by-tj-klune.html?zx=deb386e50f525d6e" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384707178i/6936447.png" width="162" height="143" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9130284153435756091">Re-Read 7/29-8/1/18 Still one of my all time favorites!!<br/><br/>5 stars is not enough!!!<br/><br/>What did I just read? This book was absolutely stunning.   <span id="freeText9130284153435756091" style="display:none">Re-Read 7/29-8/1/18 Still one of my all time favorites!!<br /><br />5 stars is not enough!!!<br /><br />What did I just read? This book was absolutely stunning. The writing, the characters, the story itself, sucks you right in.<br /><br />What do you do when you own father makes you feel worthless and tells you “You’re gonna get shit, for most of your life.” As any child would, Ox believed his father. Ox grew up thinking he was no one, nothing special. Until the day he met a beautiful boy named Joe, who jumped into his arms and into his heart, and his life would never be the same. Ox and his mother would learn what it felt like being part of a loving family, even if they are a little different. They would learn about courage and sacrifice, and maybe Ox would finally figure out he was <i>never</i> nothing special.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>”You don’t get to decide what you’re worth because you obviously don’t know. You don’t get to decide that anymore because you have no f*cking idea that you’re worth everything.”~Joe</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />I can’t tell you how much I loved this book and <b>HIGHLY</b> recommend it to everyone.</span>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1684656621" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7923666745327575732"><b>5 stars for this unique, heartbreaking, soul wrenching, but absolutely amazing story!</b><br/><br/>Re-read on January 2019 and loved it just as much as I did the first time.<br/><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"You gotta smell him and tell me why it's all candy canes and pinecones and epic and awesome."<br/><br/>"And the moon. Ah God, the moon. I wished it was full. Because full moons were my favorite kind of moons. Joe's face came and blocked it away. I decided that was okay, because I loved his face more than I could ever love the moon."<br/><br/>"We had </i></blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText7923666745327575732" style="display:none"><b>5 stars for this unique, heartbreaking, soul wrenching, but absolutely amazing story!</b><br /><br />Re-read on January 2019 and loved it just as much as I did the first time.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"You gotta smell him and tell me why it's all candy canes and pinecones and epic and awesome."<br /><br />"And the moon. Ah God, the moon. I wished it was full. Because full moons were my favorite kind of moons. Joe's face came and blocked it away. I decided that was okay, because I loved his face more than I could ever love the moon."<br /><br />"We had lived. We had loved. We had lost. Oh god, had we lost.”</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br />Oh, how I suffered for Ox and Joe, how I've though my heart won't take it anymore. <br /><br />I am only sorry that we don't get many hot scenes. This is my only complaint. I would have wanted more heated moments between Ox and Joe. But the writing is absolutely amazing and I just couldn't put it down!</span>

  <span id="freeText4703766530717519034" style="display:none">TJ Klune hates us. Wookie Cry Face, he says. We've heard him warn us of Wookie Cry Face. I say <b>BRING IT.</b> I ain't skeered of no effin Wookie Cry Face! I've tackled your Wookie Cry Face before, TJ. I am undefeated!<br><br>But after this book?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464306997ra/19225377.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously one of the worst book hangovers ever. In the best possible way. Damn him. <br><br>Ox is sixteen when he meets his future - the family just down the road. Ten (soon to be eleven-year-old) Joe climbs on his back and takes him home. And his fate is sealed.<br><br>Ox has never felt like he was worth much. But he is so, so special. Joe's family (now Ox's family) knows it. Ox's mother knows it. Ox's work family knows it. Joe, especially, knows it. <br><br>TJ takes us through many years of Ox's life. There is heartache. First because of love unrequited.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <b>"And I've been waiting," Joe said. "For him to look at me like I looked at him."</b>
  </em>
</blockquote><br><br>And then we get some cute and some happy. And some wolves! <br><br>And then........<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464306997ra/19225378.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464306997ra/19225379.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <b>Three years. One month. Twenty-six days.</b>
  </em>
</blockquote><br><br>TJ's not done yet.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464306997ra/19225380.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <b>"As long as it takes for you to decide to run again."<br><br>"....please don't make me leave."</b>
  </em>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't want you to think it's ALL crying and shredding of your heart. TJ will put you back together. But it'll have about 57,836 Bandaids on it after. Just sayin'. <br><br>Ox finds out about unexpected family. And unexpected strength. Pack doesn't have to mean wolf. That he is worth it. He's worth everything to some people. Especially his tornado. His Joe. <br><br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <b>"I would always choose you. I don't care if it's a biological imperative. I don't care if it's some destiny. I don't care if you were made specifically for me. It doesn't matter. Because I would choose you regardless."</b>
  </em>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_1776823425" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1776823425" />
    <a title="Alexandra Elend Wolf" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf"><img alt="Alexandra Elend Wolf" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587677046p2/48780241.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1776823425?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexandra Elend Wolf" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexandra Elend Wolf" href="/user/show/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf">Alexandra Elend Wolf</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/49454838-wolfsong">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf?shelf=2020">2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf?shelf=favorites-trilogies-series">favorites-trilogies-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf?shelf=uniquely-written-books">uniquely-written-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48780241-alexandra-elend-wolf?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1776823425" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8408406371010862910"><blockquote> <i> <b> “It should have been obvious. It should have been obvious what they were, but then I wasn’t looking for the incredible buried in the ordinary.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br/><br/>I love wolves. They're my favorite animal. They're majestic and beautiful, and loyal and powerful, and I could probably talk about wolves for days. So... Why the heck didn't I read this before?!<br/><br/>Seriously it's just ridiculous how much time this has been sitting in my tbr, especially since, just by the name, I knew it would involve wolves, adding the </span>
  <span id="freeText8408406371010862910" style="display:none"><blockquote> <i> <b> “It should have been obvious. It should have been obvious what they were, but then I wasn’t looking for the incredible buried in the ordinary.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br /><br />I love wolves. They're my favorite animal. They're majestic and beautiful, and loyal and powerful, and I could probably talk about wolves for days. So... Why the heck didn't I read this before?!<br /><br />Seriously it's just ridiculous how much time this has been sitting in my tbr, especially since, just by the name, I knew it would involve wolves, adding the fact that I have heard just magnificent things about it. Honestly, I'm mad at myself.<br /><br />This was such a wonderful read.<br /><br />The narration was so deep and meaningful. <b> I could taste and see and feel everything because it was described in such a way that was easy to feel. </b> The use of colors made the book so bright, and somehow all that much more specific.<br /><br /><blockquote> <i> <b> " I remembered the first time I held Joe's hand, the little tornado who said I smelled of pinecones and candy canes. Of epic and awesome." </b> </i> </blockquote><br /><br />The characters though. Oh, how I love them. They're just so <b> wonderful and expansive, full of sides, layers, and years of growth. </b> I love how every character got to play such important, meaningful parts. Each in their own ways. There was nothing wasted.<br /><br />They are all so different and merge together so seamlessly... it made my heart ache with love and that wonderful feeling of completeness and satisfaction. <br /><br />I love them all, I could probably choose a favorite character if I had to but I would seriously avoid that decision with all my might because it's just cruel. Each and everyone of them has so much <b> depth and layers and clear paths to take. </b> They all play an important part in the story and make it feel so real and full of magic. <br /><br />The book has a lot of plot to drive it BUT <b> character-driven </b> is also a very good definition for it and, probably, the most accurate as well. <br /><br /><blockquote> <i> <b> “Things are changing. They will. They have to. But you and me? I promise that won’t ever change.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br /><br /><b> Ox's </b> and <b> Joe's </b> realtionship was <b> completely adorable and wonderfully heartbreaking. </b> <br /><br />I swear, there is nothing more beautiful than a relationship that develops slowly through the passage of years and it has grown organically through all that time. Nothing. Because it lays the path to <b> a very healthy and comprehensive relationship that is strong and everlasting. </b> And these two just have one of the cutest there are. <br /><br />It's... different and so much more than either of them thought but oh so rewarding and beautiful. Not easy, no, but simple, at the end of the day, and just right. <br /><br />Everything that goes into it just makes it sweeter. <br /><br /><blockquote> <i> <b> “You’re alive. If you can take another breath, if you take another step, then you’re not broken. Battered, maybe. Bruised. Cracked. But never broken.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br /><br />The plot was... Perfect, just perfect. The whole ride was such a roller-coaster, exactly how life is. One second things were happy and, well maybe not perfect but good, and then the next everything changed. And just as fast things can tip to one side or the other.<br /><br />What I love the most is the way <b> the story takes place over a vast expansion of years </b> and we havea ll that time to see things <b> simmer and grow and just be </b> in between of all the crazy that comes with it. <br /><br />The book did many things I wasn't expecting it to do but, the wonderful thing is, <b> it never strayed from the path that we were clearly given at the beginning. </b> We are given a mysterious world but, as mysterious as it is, everything is given to us right from the beginning and there's jsut the question of how things play out. <br /><br />History has a way of repeating itself, after all, and things are more than they seem at first sight. <br /><br /><blockquote> <i> <b> “Sometimes, it’s not about being able to shift. Some of us are already born with a wolf in our heart.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br /><br />The ending was more than I could ever expect, and that's such a wonderful thing to say. I didn't know what to think about everything and I was shell-shocked, but it was wonderful - the way it was subtlety hinted in earlier chapters - and fitted right in.<br /><br />I cried (of happiness, of sadness, sometimes both), and then I would laugh, and sometimes I would be crying AND laughing at the beauty of life all at the same time. <b> And it felt perfect, it felt green. </b><br /><br />I was so engrossed with it, I picked it up and didn't want to put it back down. <b> It took a couple of lines to capture my attention, to enraptured me so absolutely that I wouldn't think of anything else. </b> And it freaking hurt to put it down in order to lead a life, I just wanted to know what happened next. And now I just want for it to continue and never end.<br /><br /><blockquote> <i> <b> “We had lived. We had loved. We had lost. Oh god, had we lost. But we would be here now. Together.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br /><blockquote> <i> <b> “Because we were the goddamn Bennett pack. And our song would always be heard.” </b> </i> </blockquote><br /><br /><s> <i> Now the revise version of the review. </i> </s><br /><br /><i> First time read: 2018/07/01<br />Second time read: 2020/09/29 </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="8408406371010862910" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2192950000" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2192950000" />
    <a title="Wil Loves Books!" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3232198-wil-loves-books"><img alt="Wil Loves Books!" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467223384p2/3232198.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2192950000?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wil Loves Books!" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wil Loves Books!" href="/user/show/3232198-wil-loves-books">Wil Loves Books!</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=on-kindle">on-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=best-of-tbr">best-of-tbr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3232198-wil-loves-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2192950000" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7202254138718085574"><b> 5 Huge Candy Canes and Pinecones and Epic and Awesome Stars!!! </b><br/><br/><br/><b> <i> “Red,” he said quietly. “Your eyes are red.” </i> </b><br/><br/>I’m struggling with words to write a review that would make this book justice. I probably can’t come up with them. This was awesome, OMG, so awesome. From beginning to end, this book captured my heart. I used to be a huge paranormal reader, not sure why I stopped reading paranormal on a regular basis, but I probably need to rectify that. But this book, man, this book, was pure amazingn</span>
  <span id="freeText7202254138718085574" style="display:none"><b> 5 Huge Candy Canes and Pinecones and Epic and Awesome Stars!!! </b><br /><br /><br /><b> <i> “Red,” he said quietly. “Your eyes are red.” </i> </b><br /><br />I’m struggling with words to write a review that would make this book justice. I probably can’t come up with them. This was awesome, OMG, so awesome. From beginning to end, this book captured my heart. I used to be a huge paranormal reader, not sure why I stopped reading paranormal on a regular basis, but I probably need to rectify that. But this book, man, this book, was pure amazingness. <br /><br /><b> <i>“Mom! Mom. You have to smell him! It’s like… like… I don’t even know what it’s like! I was walking in the woods to scope out our territory so I could be like Dad and then it was like… whoa. And then he was all standing there and he didn’t see me at first because I’m getting so good at hunting. I was all like rawr and grr but then I smelled it again and it was him and it was all kaboom! I don’t even know! I don’t even know! You gotta smell him and then tell me why it’s all candy canes and pinecones and epic and awesome.” </i></b> <br /><br />It’s such a simple, yet complex story. And such simple, yet complex characters. I had an idea about the general theme of werewolves and such, but I really didn’t know much about the plot, or the story. <br /><br /><b> <i> “And I’ve been waiting,” Joe said. “For him to look at me like I looked at him. And he finally did. He finally did. And I’m going to do everything I can to make sure it stays like that. Because I want him for always.” </i></b><br /><br />I loved all of these characters, a lot. The sense of family, the homo-eroticism of it all. And how they interacted with each other. So character driven, and so full of fun, heartbreak, and love, so much love. <br /><br /><b> <i> So he pressed his forehead against mine and breathed me in and there was that sun, okay? That sun between us, that bond that burned and burned and burned because he’d given it to me. Because he’d chosen me. And I got to choose him back. </i></b> <br /><br /><b> <i> He was beautiful because he was Joe. He was beautiful because he was mine. </i></b> <br /><br /><br /> And Ox. Ox. Ox. And Joe. Joe. Joe. <br /><br /><b> <i> There was never anyone such as him before. From that little boy on the road, to the teenager with red eyes, to the hardened man who stood before me at the house at the end of the lane and said the same words he’d said to me all those years before. There was never one like him. And he was mine. </i></b> <br /><br /><b> <i> That’s what life is, Ox. Choices. The choices we make shape what we’ll become. For a long time, Joe’s choices were taken from him. And then they were ruled by fear. But you came along and he made his own choice. So yes. I could have stopped him. I could have told him to wait. I could have told him no. But I didn’t because he chose. He chose you, Ox.” </i></b> <br /><br /><br />This is such an epic story, not just a love story, an epic story overall that spans many years. I won't even attempt to explain to you this story, but just trust me when I say that, well, it was just perfection. I don’t think I can say anything else because, again, I have no words. This is my first TJ Klune read and it definitely won’t be my last. This one gave me all the feels, and then some. Top favorite this year. Can’t wait for Ravensong!<br /><br /><b> <i> He said, “Oh my god.” <br />He said, “Ox.” <br />He said, “Ox, can you feel it? This is—I can’t believe we—after all this time we—” <br />He said, “Ox.” <br />He said, “Mate.” <br />The wolf snarled, “Mine.” </i></b> </span>
  <a data-text-id="7202254138718085574" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_1646182104" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1646182104" />
    <a title="Mary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3142827-mary"><img alt="Mary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473696269p2/3142827.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1646182104?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary" href="/user/show/3142827-mary">Mary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3142827-mary?shelf=own-it">own-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3142827-mary?shelf=paperback-is-mine">paperback-is-mine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3142827-mary?shelf=keeper">keeper</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3142827-mary?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1646182104" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer742021862483904479">It's a flawless book and shows that you can take the fantastic and make it so very human. Ox is so well named, solid and sturdy with everything swirling around him, he is the linchpin that holds everyone together. I thought the supernatural would be what grabbed me but instead it's Ox's humanity and humility and loyalty. I hope there will be more. Wildly recommended. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('27xOaY3qJnKu/jKUmkJXV3JO9mprvGHFM1SZ8xLs/NbTgqOZ7+syU+QTkxEfeRfQoWXfnoAgtejCqFBeF2R4eQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZXZ0lLRXHsRQiwn1nxUOtPezT7ZY2BpHeBlir/ZKJP9tSJlk1lYK5RpmqHAaLk4zJJhmQrNEzmqJ5asC88KgUA==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3711146228756366839">TJ KLUNE is a Lambda Literary Award-winning author (Into This River I Drown) and an ex-claims examiner for an insurance company. His novels include The House in the Cerulean Sea and The Extraordinaries. Being queer himself, TJ believes it's important—now more than ever—to have accurate, positive, queer representation in stories.</span>
